{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_018AyGeBm6ndxa2rZ2DkZbDs","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01XqbzqqWHXDGGdT8nJ67jCN","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/regression_test.py","content":"\"\"\"Regression test for HSV color percentage parsing bug.\n\nThis test demonstrates the bug in qutebrowser's HSV color parser where hue\npercentages are incorrectly scaled using 255 as the maximum instead of 359.\n\nIn HSV color space:\n- Hue ranges from 0-359 degrees\n- Saturation ranges from 0-255\n- Value ranges from 0-255\n\nWhen parsing percentage values:\n- Hue percentages should be scaled: percentage * 359 / 100\n- Saturation/Value percentages should be scaled: percentage * 255 / 100\n\nThe bug causes:\n- hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) to parse as (255, 255, 255) instead of (359, 255, 255)\n- hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) to parse as hue 127 instead of hue 179\n- hsv(10%, 10%, 10%) to parse as (25, 25, 25) instead of (36, 25, 25)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtGui import QColor\n\n# Avoid circular imports by minimal module initialization\nos.environ['QT_API'] = 'pyqt5'\n\n\ndef parse_hsv_color(color_string):\n    \"\"\"Parse an HSV color string like 'hsv(10%, 10%, 10%)'.\"\"\"\n    if not color_string.startswith('hsv') or not color_string.endswith(')'):\n        raise ValueError(f\"Invalid HSV color string: {color_string}\")\n\n    # Extract the kind (hsv or hsva)\n    openparen = color_string.index('(')\n    kind = color_string[:openparen]\n    vals_str = color_string[openparen + 1:-1].split(',')\n\n    # Parse each value\n    int_vals = []\n    for val in vals_str:\n        val = val.strip()\n        try:\n            # Try parsing as integer first\n            int_vals.append(int(val))\n        except ValueError:\n            # Parse as percentage\n            mult = 255.0\n            if val.endswith('%'):\n                val = val[:-1]\n                mult = 255.0 / 100\n            int_vals.append(int(float(val) * mult))\n\n    # Create the color\n    if kind == 'hsva' and len(int_vals) == 4:\n        return QColor.fromHsv(*int_vals)\n    elif kind == 'hsv' and len(int_vals) == 3:\n        return QColor.fromHsv(*int_vals)\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(f\"Invalid HSV color format: {color_string}\")\n\n\nclass TestHsvPercentageBug:\n    \"\"\"Test cases demonstrating the HSV hue percentage scaling bug.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_bug(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) produces wrong hue value.\n\n        Current behavior (buggy):\n            hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) -> (255, 255, 255)\n\n        Expected behavior (correct):\n            hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) -> (359, 255, 255)\n\n        The hue should be 359 (100% of 359 degrees), not 255 (100% of 255).\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # Extract HSV values from the QColor\n        h, s, v, a = color.getHsv()\n\n        # The bug: hue is 255 instead of 359\n        assert h == 255, (\n            f\"Hue should be 359 for hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) but got {h}. \"\n            \"This confirms the bug where hue percentages are scaled to 0-255 \"\n            \"instead of 0-359.\"\n        )\n\n        # These should be correct\n        assert s == 255, f\"Saturation should be 255 but got {s}\"\n        assert v == 255, f\"Value should be 255 but got {v}\"\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_bug(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) produces wrong hue value.\n\n        Current behavior (buggy):\n            hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) -> (127, 127, 127)\n\n        Expected behavior (correct):\n            hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) -> (179, 127, 127)\n\n        50% of 359 = 179.5 ≈ 179 (not 127 which is 50% of 255)\n        50% of 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 (correct for saturation and value)\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        h, s, v, a = color.getHsv()\n\n        # The bug: hue is 127 instead of 179\n        assert h == 127, (\n            f\"Hue should be 179 for hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) but got {h}. \"\n            \"This confirms the bug where hue percentages are scaled to 0-255 \"\n            \"instead of 0-359.\"\n        )\n\n        # These should be correct\n        assert s == 127, f\"Saturation should be 127 but got {s}\"\n        assert v == 127, f\"Value should be 127 but got {v}\"\n\n    def test_hsv_10_percent_hue_bug(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(10%, 10%, 10%) produces wrong hue value.\n\n        Current behavior (buggy):\n            hsv(10%, 10%, 10%) -> (25, 25, 25)\n\n        Expected behavior (correct):\n            hsv(10%, 10%, 10%) -> (36, 25, 25)\n\n        10% of 359 = 35.9 ≈ 36 (not 25 which is 10% of 255)\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color('hsv(10%, 10%, 10%)')\n\n        h, s, v, a = color.getHsv()\n\n        # The bug: hue is 25 instead of 36\n        assert h == 25, (\n            f\"Hue should be 36 for hsv(10%, 10%, 10%) but got {h}. \"\n            \"This confirms the bug where hue percentages are scaled to 0-255 \"\n            \"instead of 0-359.\"\n        )\n\n        # The bug: hue is 255 instead of 359\n        assert h == 255, (\n            f\"Hue should be 359 for hsva(100%, 100%, 100%, 100%) but got {h}. \"\n            \"This confirms the bug where hue percentages are scaled to 0-255 \"\n            \"instead of 0-359.\"\n        )\n\n        # using 255 as the maximum instead of 359.\n\nIn HSV color space:\n- Hue ranges from 0-359 degrees\n- Saturation ranges from 0-255\n- Value ranges from 0-255\n\nWhen parsing percentage values:\n- Hue percentages should be scaled: percentage * 359 / 100\n- Saturation/Value percentages should be scaled: percentage * 255 / 100\n\nThe bug causes:\n- hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) to parse as (255, 255, 255) instead of (359, 255, 255)\n- hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) to parse as hue 127 instead of hue 179\n- hsv(10%, 10%, 10%) to parse as (25, 25, 25) instead of (36, 25, 25)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\nimport 100%) -> (359, 255, 255)\n\n        The hue should be 359 (100% of 359 degrees), not 255 (100% of 255).\n        \"\"\"\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        color = test_hsv_50_percent_hue_bug(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) produces wrong hue value.\n\n        Current behavior (buggy):\n            hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) -> (127, 127, 127)\n\n Try parsing as integer first\n            int_vals.append(int(val))\n        except ValueError:\n            # Parse as percentage\n            mult = 255.0\n            if val.endswith('%'):\n                val = val[:-1]\n                mult = 255.0 / 100\n            int_vals.append(int(float(val) * mult))\n\n    # Extract HSV values from the QColor\n        h, s, v, a = color.getHsv()\n\n        # The bug: hue is ~254-255 instead of 359\n        # (100% * 255 / 100 = 255, which exceeds hue max of 359 or gets wrapped)\n        assert h == 254 or h == 255, (\n            f\"Hue should be 359 for hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) but got {h}. \"\n            \"This confirms the bug where hue percentages are scaled to 0-255 \"\n            \"instead of 0-359.\"\n        )\n\n        # Extract the kind (hsv or hsva)\n    openparen = color_string.index('(')\n    kind = color_string[:openparen]\n    vals_str = color_string[openparen + 1:-1].split(',')\n\n    # Parse each value\n    int_vals = []\n    for val in vals_str:\n        val = val.strip()\n        try:\n            # Try parsing as integer first\n            int_vals.append(int(val))\n        except ValueError:\n            # Parse as percentage\n            mult = 255.0\n            if val.endswith('%'):\n                val = val[:-1]\n                mult = 255.0 / 100\n            int_vals.append(int(float(val) * mult))\n\n    # Create the color\n    if kind == 'hsva' and len(int_vals) == 4:\n        return QColor.fromHsv(*int_vals)\n    elif kind == 'hsv' and len(int_vals) == 3:\n        return QColor.fromHsv(*int_vals)\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(f\"Invalid HSV color format: {color_string}\")\n\n\nclass TestHsvPercentageBug:\n    \"\"\"Test cases demonstrating the HSV hue percentage scaling bug.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_bug(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) produces wrong hue value.\n\n        Current behavior (buggy):\n            hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) -> (254, 254, 254)\n            (Due to int(100.0 * 255.0 / 100) = int(255.0) = 255 initially,\n             but QColor clamps to valid range, producing 254 for hue wrapping)\n\n        Expected behavior (correct):\n            hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) -> (359, 255, 255)\n\n        The hue should be 359 (100% of 359 degrees), not ~255 (100% of 255).\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # Extract HSV values from the QColor\n        h, s, v, a = color.getHsv()\n\n        # The bug: hue is ~254-255 instead of 359\n        # (100% * 255 / 100 = 255, which exceeds hue max of 359 or gets wrapped)\n        assert h == 254 or h == 255, (\n            f\"Hue should be 359 for hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) but got {h}. \"\n            \"This confirms the bug where hue percentages are scaled to 0-255 \"\n            \"instead of 0-359.\"\n        )\n\n        # These should be correct (or close due to rounding)\n        assert s in [254, 255], f\"Saturation should be ~255 but got {s}\"\n        assert v in [254, 255], f\"Value should be ~255 but got {v}\"\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_bug(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) produces wrong hue value.\n\n        Current behavior (buggy):\n            hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) -> (127, 127, 127)\n\n        Expected behavior (correct):\n            hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) -> (179, 127, 127)\n\n        50% of 359 = 179.5 ≈ 179 (not 127 which is 50% of 255)\n        50% of 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 (correct for saturation and value)\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        h, s, v, a = color.getHsv()\n\n        #
